Media Riptide

 

You may want to set aside next weekend for this. Nieman Journalism Lab <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lfAKi4GsyEefkTWx9ssLQCXwaU1k_DXdyldZ1kKGcgPDv-9cx66nO2bYwn7v-7BqgNq8TEXJtSOQSJD9cUv8aEO-ptsbLvTeQ_UaRA_HwmluE5-lPgB-5g==>  has released a tome called "Riptide," chronicling media's transformation brought on by digital in the past 30+ years. Among the many media honchos, Business Insider's Henry Blodget is positioned as a disruptor and he's asked about whether programmatic media is an opportunity or not by interviewer and former NY Times exec Martin Nisenholtz. He replies, "What programmatic has allowed us to do is now raise the value of [commodity banner ads] a lot, so it's helping us. Industrywide, what you're going to see is the programmatics or the automated buying and more efficient buying is going to drive down pricing for advertising. That is OK for us, because we have built the model to be able to do fine on ad rates that are considerably below the current average across the industry." Read Blodget's interview <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lfAKi4GsyEeZmPnr1jRpp6rtP5jjpfQiaEiEH9djYiai-gQx0kmNkH-pde7DDCkGf0Ddf6Re1o2yukQO57vLMU7MIU1XLqB3R3pKKvJj9V9N04MSKngvaD7z2ppHcT51_ls4-6BjFkav7UyTMHGvznyesaQhwKn4A2iHxmyoCJ4=> . And read Riptide next weekend <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lfAKi4GsyEcYiX3504bIZ0CVrLcJpQJVf2CXnTMGXK8mllEM47cZ3snFcC_uoFuYTEXaFnXRJJYqKfOwvo69moBWGOz9ZCAoNSFRfRpKoftRQOMLk7c8yBEjWfMYiKzkuFFaLOgJWSc=> .

 

Reaching In Mobile

 

ComScore released its July 2013 stats for reach among smartphone sites and apps in the U.S. on Friday with Google and Facebook topping the list with about 90% reach. See it. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lfAKi4GsyEcmvv0AeKuwnKFel-Y-yessFnJQtY_mPPPXjtsDTMLC22Br7xK5qnXdVDyp_BQcGopsoAShjWy4im3YNq1N1Tl8EdtfoI00-sNtZu68Qpp6nEmYV1Tjh0tl1qPpLx1ZmBewsOJ5OO9FCDxRt-pLFei91eOwe3gUfYY1UkjfC35fAI34JWL9-Pb5aJAmBEk91WT9Wh_M5YLePKxMvbpBlES8ddaPp5oWrt3Q-z5n2RkPBbu3fepv6i9G>  Of note, The Weather Company has more reach than Twitter, according to comScore.

 

Data Don't Lie

 

Digiday's Jack Marshall details a man vs. machine story around digital ad sales. He writes about Dutch morning newspaper De Telegraaf, which "makes its salespeople compete directly with programmatic channels, and it factors things like salaries and other overheads into its ad decisions. This is yield management taken to the extreme. If the paper can make more money selling ads through exchanges or other programmatic deals for a $4 CPM than it does from direct deals for $8, it'll do that instead. As the philosopher Rasheed Wallace might put it: Data don't lie." Read it <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lfAKi4GsyEcfbGxvTPsCeK85D0bCAPiKY0IhihBlPeRmZ2bRhtoWwHPuejncfUEGBsExqWuuDgC7Ab2FcmZp0Mv93FVgOVgBPf3uSJBmF2Bo6sJn5FOqHfe6G5isUoqp4lcswmCvK9kC8p4DO4nGbw==> .

 

Consumer Data

 

On FT.com, Emily Steel looks at new efforts (AboutTheData.com <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lfAKi4GsyEf4q7uEIY2dtiYEPWOnjXmk--ub7f5q5OCq1JWRvea5GCmHNKIevzUaksZlc1teMJiNxTGfbopg04K9q4t4ZssTjFyOY5rmrFFHz6ccDRZ_-Q==> ) by Acxiom to show users what data Acxiom and its clients have on them. Steel says the plan is backfiring according to several consumer privacy advocates, including Center for Digital Democracy's Jeff Chester and the ACLU's Christopher Sogohian. She summarizes, "Critics said that the data Acxiom discloses through the site is only a small sample of the information the company tracks and sells and does not include more sensitive categories, such as propensity for gambling or likelihood of smoking." Read more (subscription) <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lfAKi4GsyEe4EpuWqT2_g4AvlEH2q3cykl0rlUCf0z5Y8UuvEZXG6gX_DkdH3DPp_nufiRACs-k8u1Pi9FzaMh1vciWYf00Dw0qziPfNCVmfaRE-AqEYZ7kKGm3wUizkomHgf2vOCX6N3W0yXpa4hgGxIHTKaih-ffAHXUSqxhwT3-hShwgXCAmnADOeOk4h> .

 

Yahoo Upfront

 

Yahoo is following AOL's lead and pitching advertisers on a programmatic upfront, albeit much more quietly. According to Ad Age's Tim Peterson, advertisers want to do business with Yahoo, but they are concerned about pricing and Yahoo's outdated ad technology. "One of the challenges is how they funnel Yahoo owned-and-operated [inventory] into RMX," an agency exec said. "I don't think it's changed in five years. As much as they talk about upgrading, from what we're seeing the infrastructure is outdated." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lfAKi4GsyEe78IQ2pvKp-yazXmjX_mBAokBPVT6e_QxOLdQ-8BJ_5chmtvOq_G4uaeCyHjAlQgNjUsqgs0zOTNxrJlhBDBEo2vWmQ8S-BLgHUTa5JM2BShDwChpQZSmW2kE4nbQNDmkKn2k5Nexs7rWDilHkaxxGf9gygpANqO16j9IxMtj0sFVbE5T4nfYLePMKPpIi0wM=> .

Analytics Funding

 

Analytics startup AdYapper raised $1.2 million in seed funding led by KGC Capital, TechCrunch is reporting. The company seeks to add more depth to analytics through proprietary metrics such as viewable click-through rate, rather than regular click-through rate, and brand exposure duration. "[Clients need] the data delivered real-time via API for RTB, programmatic buying, and attribution modeling, as well as clear action items presented in a beautiful UI, in one format, not just numbers on a page," said CEO and founder Elliot Hirsch. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lfAKi4GsyEf2sfd1QQWTIaotxeGqjY4ilb4Fk5IFuiBZwZTygfxUNE0d1CFSdzt4DI4TPY2tyfVyjpwpS-FC9mqbNLvOSzALcxhsh53DyDZbhMj9UQPP55o-IZzXKI4fxGE2DoOTsHj4WWbBdr43z1NFsUaDq9r4hiyPig1LDjP9VPm418Pbd2SWEkgrs87yGLRiwJzwcd0v9C-dDUh9TZvZk3IfFq8CVNzrvMg-cS7ymSgtL7VDJQ==> .

 

Flight Data

 

Delta Airlines is taking a step in the more personalized flight direction by giving flight attendants smartphones to handle food and drink sales, as well as seat upgrades. As Businessweek points out, there is a part of this new process that will lead to flight attendants using "customer-specific information to enable more personalized service." The one caveat will be avoiding the creepiness factor. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lfAKi4GsyEczsnwm_STDdAVcwiyyocMgJhGG9Aq-J0i3II7omu-w-nSPQn4J1Q0n-vjB5iGuqP-ZrHficZ5IV5scW6kEPAfl2m8YeJBi8V7Ata9QaZ4--k-xQ4z3rDvSg06Zw90LbiJJcvIEL5_vEdcpIAOr6zcipWebZQkmcX2cSmqmft_zf7FWYetWDXnI2gpzW0vYvp9QMoT1_MwCLTyV7ZW_8RNm> .

 

The Big "Pivot"

 

ChoiceStream's recommendation software worked well, but the market wasn't big enough, says ChoiceStream. So the company "pivoted" a bit to bring its recommendation algorithms to programmatic advertising -- that's according to the Boston Business Journal, which talked to ChoiceStream CEO Eric Bosco about the transition the company has made over the last 13 years. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lfAKi4GsyEd3h0dhaAX6Z-sjU6aurnOBLYkHt5KbEHn09FSEl2uxPpUJhm9xPU64siBEzD3_EOupbwaOfFOYSoLdJ5X7eMRDuh8ngugIJCTZQPPQsIHeX5xq3JDJX0Hjptr5sqjmR5D98qk9yAId5g_UgP0Q6qwSwjlgM_19wATfkfiDM0WhJnvNrGw5nocwF64KCgSeScB0_8Lki7PgIxZBxxFv8tZgsxAtNko_ziY1kNa4_CqTig==> . The company has raised more than $78 million in its lifetime.

 

Mobile Imps, Hits

 

Mobile-ad firm Millennial Media released its Mobile Mix report for Q2 2013, with findings similar to Q1. Some of the notable points are that the report now includes tablets and other connected devices as well as smartphones and feature phones. Apple remains the top manufacturer for mobile impressions, with Samsung coming in second. Amazon shows up on the list of top manufacturers, despite not being a true hardware company, due to its Amazon Kindle. Android remains the largest operating system for smartphones. Read the report here (pay with some PII) <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lfAKi4GsyEeey9kzVULg-1Wh-2nvbkOhLrEUG7v0wuQfqTpoLAjMPILjMQbA1qmqaIkBOy539K0TrzFRh2mQPD4JytDzlQ3uP7l81-Fn7t1YLAs5EK5r0lEugCtqZt431oXX4PHTsxxiNlfpOWAbtEavbBhPApP0rvtzvY662UzVzYaWj9TiiA==> . And, Apple continues to dominate the tablet market.

 

Compensating The Agent

 

On The Makegood, Underscore Marketing's Tom Hespos argues that changes in agency compensation models are inevitable. He counsels marketers, "Look for strategic counsel to become a hot commodity in the coming years, and be sure that when compensation models are discussed with potential clients, your agency comes down on the right side for what you hope to accomplish over the course of the relationship." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lfAKi4GsyEd8x_OGMf7TcdtkBWgV6m9rFjAK01q1YJJfqdeMPOyr9ZksvdNuwrNHytJoxQ758CEVkz7k-_Vg3OkXHD7V9W_uuSyM8o0GdIlR7uWNgjqCVLBi2GWMCXBbLjm8Zn6WZ-iZpFcaZ0AbCwmp7g0299Mwp-zmrrPmk439sxupaVDXaboUSl4ZSjoIAdh0Tu-QDOc=> .

 

For "Native" Marketers

 

According to TechCrunch, Outbrain and Taboola have a new competitor called Ideal Media. The company evidently provides content recommendation units along with custom "native" integrations and other content-marketing capabilities. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lfAKi4GsyEe-16aFsd5XH4jj3uqDSZClOJzQTw2zwLzlKs7pjGAgYBAZFZUH9Bs67TJWuOzDBxZGmKO1OubQ5tGYSZiMo0kUzZ_4jVGN42o0hF0xkyw25lEsrWlA6R4Zb46qAK9tf59lOCScYTyWgRVpNFLjZqMBZJJlNFXv_up7HV9pCzIcsRu3W9q86M8Dih5vQuZiDLvgbNCWycScdJ6vdqMlcT9vPzRaTWnkMls6irWx72q0FmUcE0oUxZIi> .

 

Buying Big Data

 

Swiss advertising platform Adello Group has acquired big data startup HStreaming, according to GigaOM. Although HStreaming was doing well, it was hard to scale. "The technology has no practical limitations, but we have to market the company. ... Watch what happens in the next six months. ... I sold 800 customers at Vertica before I sold the company [to HP], and every one of them is going to want HStreaming," said Chris Lynch of Atlas Venture, an HStreaming investor. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lfAKi4GsyEfSU2kTG0YWLNTo1UK0cFwytc6_4MxiZfdSx3Y7z9XXBDEMDfJN5rZ0tAcY0SpF5UdcMe0P5PI_htYshDyV99S5XEiaqx_i7Yxv2dSCc6XsyUSVCkZPYPBq_g139lxNZn7Xh_Ew92QJiajSS1Tqri-t43fJPjqu6jYJWZKfC2p6wh7QNCTh7-oG9VRhyQ1zaoU=> .

New Product, Old Partners

 

SAP and Accenture are continuing their partnership, this time by offering a product aimed at CMOs to "easily view and act on centralized key marketing performance data such as sales figures, media spend and social reach in near real-time." Accenture will be the single point of contact for services running on the HANA platform, simplifying the process. The new CMO product, called the Marketing Performance Solution, will initially be targeted at retail and consumer packaged-goods customers. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001s3r8H617w29wbyf2NBOvf5n-sQOT2G1t3Gd7CGXuuDwSSO-tArqWP7YuC-324WTbZBaSfHfdFw5qROnNK4ol0cSoDF-7rwQlYkOAj9rqfgqs6atVT1Nd7OJH9ZGrmqdcnaMkzONODiBLDspTsfygwLTjyDoCMxsbnMs4U0YP5my-dmeQ4yGdfE1kjTnPp2rkxXIoeclm7GU-i6DB6gDZDf-qdXDrhQpA3vfDjWMzNN8pPyPiLrfjWePvp9hXxzZFBVtU5KqksNVfAev9KIqvJRiZWXyHdZzmQHHo5GOK9zw=> .

 

Retail Domination

 

Retail dominates as the largest spender in digital media, according to an eMarketer report. Retail represents 22.3% of the total US digital advertising spending share; financial services comes in second at 12.4%. Within the retail industry, direct response makes up 64.6% of paid media -- a lot of it channeled into SEM. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001s3r8H617w2_NYILVTawdBbvcEyFgMfmxbyeK01rw2oP7guQu7A0XOb926J5wVcPiQsi6km2pqSi1qX-flcgMQgo9WhtH51L_n3iBVcuvrHq4HvPI2gyCNzY-CmlM62Q-U_qWADas1_n0Vcmz677167dh3hVTMf7Z0u4jeklosBXXOdsN3znn7-dffum3H1DNfRuUtlxTAKB9_SQOvg8C0xqtqaIZzeWrlhzfyzH9VfU=> .

 

Retail TV

 

TV ratings are typically tied to how many people watched a particular show, but Placed decided to take it further and analyze how viewing habits relate to retail in its "Ratings to Retail - Fall TV 2013." The study found that 43% of respondents watched TV on their smartphone, which was more than computers and tablets. The study also found that viewers of all the major TV networks were more likely to visit movie theaters. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001s3r8H617w29_LpBy9Zeu3a9vllUndtIH_TJ_eU1RmR5AD-lKQuQ-d2qQkGPlFoLf5vZPekWj74cOEijymE5Y23Cl4-Rta6OKQdpqqi0HiT1jfpDhzyAKmL0zmhVfS9TruOM6mXcDPqxjKDFoqUGb7IDI3Cvm7cEkCZZCzqKxswYhXAxTK82H1A==> .

 

New Insights

 

Marketing-automation firm Marketo has teamed up with Google on a new AdWords feature that allows marketers to track when clicks on their AdWords ads result in leads or sales in the offline world. "Marketers can use this information to adjust bids for different keywords, locations, times of day and audience segments to improve the AdWords results for the outcomes they care about," wrote Marketo marketing VP and co-founder Jon Miller in a blog post <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001s3r8H617w28mWeSjXQLuGaYsaF5lbzKlvDXyILHzxasi08ENWDE0Wn32RQ3g4kDu-GSkXeMrl5Wgfhy8xv654aQzNhWawl5TNQg86NnoY1ETQWilleMuoN_7XDGMPe4S8QODJ5_MHGgT4L7rD9s-z2zMzTP6ktgIYQwEmeKazL8d4yg9vrjlzNytyNW4He5L1ldHK__v5I5r1HPodoMN73qkikrbtgQoofyd423LAKXk2LhbrQkFWjD0O-wxb_78> . Marketo also announced a partnership with B2B targeting and personalization platform Demandbase. Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001s3r8H617w29jn6FviaS85G34JbIo2unnihdgE_HLcaNASDXIZCjvSwfaJXsAGBblLwFGydqjCimfLY1SjU70pyCn-OwiiUZ6MxTCPjAa9kHYafdNhqX5ze0-q6FMX1ikT6ow3wHlx34IpUdaP_w-B8_JxJnyv6ekim-0pubuRtVEEH1gehQ8hqRJ2sosT0I4-i-ZcrMt2rXP7TEIkma9-VNJwwgZEiJg5o1UWQkboH2f4mSdjG-tacEZjCwRknvu48IKZCNu1ohWMSMV6XAfz-ohMolztb1GO5c4JIFNTebcQKzUb8FSy0GDfS4lPAXK_QictQ5w2rg=> 

 

Data University

 

In order to nurture the next generation of college students, companies are turning to universities to train students right out of the gate on data analytics and the like. The latest company to jump on this trend, according to Ad Age <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001s3r8H617w29t-k9VsHw_1gNkAFhZfTyhvFkdIW0n1SkhOkAmIxoE3Ow7XqL5GoKTK3ZCkfpykqYbfZl1QLdAbgrbobS-H8DN5iPJq0gCjxnvpMgpsZAohFsIyj0cZSbUnUW551LSepL_LTnLBwSgkQ4VPOWgROBIVJhfMVoYJQKtGFa5ixrGKc1mXFCHj93kQUqIzajOaNpv9rMJBisPiA==> , is A-B InBev, which will be opening its Bud Lab at the University of Illinois. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001s3r8H617w2-XbbQQNylVwqKVGRHUm6ckUwjQHiff-M74Ok_jpf7vMB4amIZ_5263lWjN0OaFnAkpJLmnLgW9nXeKLHX64-Ib6b4BiLO9tELNRTQBeEDTidfNzGEl77UcEAGKPIW1iC_tqkiJ9cR2skjKhNxSCha7hBFmO5fIlzM=> .

Time's Subscriber Data

 

After a successful run with Toyota, Time Inc. hopes to capture more brands with its Engage product, which already counts Johnson & Johnson as a customer. According to Ad Age, Time Engage takes subscriber data and applies it to Web and print ads, while using data from the brand as well. "It had the overlay of much deeper lifestyle information than just general demographics," said John Lisko, executive communications director at Saatchi LA. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001DPepxCE3aYyIAdagRoe2r-M_uEu97ayU-LVrBmQJonPdyGfvC7BFYQQUl7jrjiVWhlT0GuwAGkw1lKCD-VmqfVQubkAd21JZ87dXm8ILzIX34lnD_mCQz0ZQMuPk8YLyH9OPTvEoorRNO-8hnPydD-fsf3T47_b8y3y8yBd-nVzMGtEC8-I2QoV70lV8q1pLkEExdujZRfg=> .

 

Under The Yahoo Microscope

 

Marissa Mayer gets a lot of attention, but what about Yahoo COO Henrique de Castro, who should be helping to bolster Yahoo's ad product given the relative strength of the market? As Adweek points out, it could be trouble for the former Googler, with rumors swirling that he could be let go at the end of the year if performance doesn't pick up. A lack of a programmatic strategy is cited as a possible cause by an anonymous analyst. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001DPepxCE3aYyrJz46hsXXc-vHGFxKiPvY1kHb_qPX5mr6ELxju2GlYsy2YIJe8NLyCUAmCORzrMKDDiNATYd10Z53XtAYUqHMbcX-8F2qJnSuiClGN_7liJHiZ7myl4UYWnQf35o8i6rVpRSwNFkuiGE8QD1_mZuMPbyRKlipkUBADcq0CbfRFJY9RWcX2tvSw77TlVEuYTs=> .

 

Problematic Video

 

AOL's acquisition of Adap.tv came at a time when online video was heating up, and as programmatic becomes a norm in advertising, but that doesn't mean it's problem-free. The Guardian notes there is always the risk of bogus traffic, as is the case with any automated buying in the marketplace. "I'd say that the report does AOL a favour because they now know there is an issue," Alan King says. "They can plug the holes and add an extra layer of protection to the platform." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001DPepxCE3aYysJRYfG3bw04eCY_1etqvVEE-FvwlMtWpWE-qQSblBQxTj5my27x3AAflQ2NlV2FOI7c0_Iv7EZ9gr15xuSXjgTIWbh7ecQ4yxSCzOJOhUykjIWl7BM2zCNyhD1-4XId37Y2hd5dqvgYYHqx_0ovv1P6dkWSebtufGIGQkIqqgjNhpsYgDj2CJDOp90fXNr82fNIl3Xvfo-rWTOrQdVapFbYcbAHth23LPW_y981nJgw==> .

 

New Facebook Policy

 

After a lawsuit settlement, Facebook has outlined the ways it collects and uses data on its site in an update to its Site Governance document <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001DPepxCE3aYwMbutI8SheCW2_M4A_Avvnpcq-dvrWhnUGAHfG_PlgolLSiZosKNXDrY-_4986cVOxZNmd0UFiDOMJq3MbNODd-lKtR0bLEWxpo5Z0o0yUj1NxF8KiXkjMOs0DawVZHJPPiDpfekQ0uCGw3o-zXKdx7Mfpox90kVxVu47kYcchBYA3qxSkpWcx-r0_cdql91XqtZtCywDi9eYxwyzPE82X0ay_JnA9Lo-oP67gpzhKHZRmEuL23k6Q> . Search Engine Watch grabbed an excerpt of some of the changes to the policy and a screenshot of user reactions, which are predictably pretty negative. Facebook is giving users a few days to respond to the changes before they go into effect, at which point it will be unequivocally clear that Facebook owns everything posted to its site or gathered from a third party. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001DPepxCE3aYz3QmrDcqyCIl8Eq81jqLpBqgXAi6ev50VMEORxODZ35GBGRM45iVCH5Ja-HlFByFMkmbVNu4frw-xur4VNRlk1d1XRaH4qd-4TioLpz4DDZQxz9uTFjazs5LReCgfDRUZcfUtVxdj27oIzK3TbMot6ySBHPfTjknzT3GH1YxTUC27pwMG7QmIAMpBTJytIvo11P-M4nGU-Ilvzu2mhWUuNPeutapE1yJI=> .

 

Unrecommend

 

Taboola is employing users to actively clean out bad recomendations from its platform with its new "Taboola Choices" option. An "X" will appear in the right corner of a video or article and, if the user choses to close it, a list of reasons pops up to give editors a better understanding of why it was blocked. As Videonuze points out, this is especially important for video because it often has a higher production cost, making ROI more difficult. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001DPepxCE3aYw4wka9AgHos2eXTiDk2DGOHb3n9-T4pQuTCwPpivUc24N3S6M9nEw7fo51dLFdWn9GOcZfvWYP109enbY9dfteCSLSnROTk5hFyWfdlT6oleM7iDCmJmCzJVqlDQsLuU1vFtTSNBsfOsc3-bVAjChlPDy_bIGjNOm2vpBBOqWgvpXUunX34UMfloBf6zqDXwNU-SYrmUlxvnKweNFlydSy> .

Interactive Answers

 

Answers (a.k.a. Answers.com) continues to make acquisitions, according to AllThingsD's Peter Kafka. Software company Easy2 Technologies is the latest purchase. The company's tech allows brands and retailers to create interactive features for product listings. No official word was given on the price, but Kafka estimates it at less than $20 million. 31.2 Million Mobile Video Ads

 

As part of its quarterly reporting efforts, TubeMogul examined the way users interact with mobile devices and found that users are on their phones and tablets during primetime, even more than they are on desktops. Although there are small differences in iOS and Android users, they are pretty much on par with each other in terms of consumption habits. TubeMogul estimates there are 31.2 million mobile video ads available for programmatic buying in the US. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001DPepxCE3aYxBsjjohBJNinuXLekTeYyQy82TkVs6I2zQO0HzVXB0Wy5JR1b018MnLVx31ZLBqLic635q_C0Ymd9sCoxxgfXYbZuHCtbb1bGdCpHdW-gafl4thUtEmXJiCOtUfrJIRIOqk-FiIqT7QQ==> .

Trading Desk Expansion

 

Publicis' VivaKi is continuing its international expansion and opening a regional Activation Centre in Singapore, according to Campaign Asia. This is the second VivaKi Activation Centre, the first being in Amsterdam, with a third being planned for China. Grace Liau will head up the new center as regional general manager, reporting to VivaKi President Kurt Unkel, and will be working alongside Stephen Tompkins, AOD Director. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0013hMI1i75d7XJNkRAufll3hDE3UhWqV5d9faG3yklg78EEgt7RhXkqvOZKN577AdPIAJFkwTK3lX6PhTVw5DHBjZKVtLyHUUqkubEaKAz8SHO4d35E8JbwlFa-EENrFQcG6mgVxO-SDRwhIfxrp3PA-qyc0EyeUE7j2whlfVvW46aXWRb04wz3jVab9ELDE9IiDaK7sEYxmNDrNM9fdpZAI7YNE-lVwqw3NL3jZsmM-CA-xJ2AM2v9UQYvKP319E9> . In June, prior to the Publicis-Omnicom merger <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0013hMI1i75d7U4SwKWa_-_nz3EUrXyNShhmJSxMaDlJUGElyk0YbJdL_5ilfR6CvADpnYKr5F1UKiveWAqtKGi5nAAyALrGEwXTzZIBkPEgxw7sipudC7a_ERm_49SeuyvtvDzmaf_l5bv_J9RN1_glmcHyw3P7eQtis5UAnVQT-_z04VL6NlI1SrXwQAukmO8WIhGY7fccZ_6YwWrnwUdiSE7JTmQy5f2Sp9_6Chu2crgcSouYpxPuw==> , new partner Omnicom Accuen told AdExchanger it was already seeing "tremendous success in Asia." Read it <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0013hMI1i75d7WCrliP0Jc_sEpaRPx-34beuulyEVCv6M05-2gcDiADXtu7Vr60jf65rW_aBMaszu__K7w5LJ62lt0AKQeGSL7exDDPgny74uFdxX5TMcKVBlWV8TIOEVJ4wDvU1zSazEWHhud0hjVVBX0rGV6_B-9_d3b6-aqqcFvVV2Xnoe8KCi-vCzitPG6fj2Mt4cpVXCXw-MX_RnfChwzwSrkeIRDyKKVIfgxDBvaZYv0_iNRjAg==> . Landscape Of Intent

 

Intent is everywhere, at least according to KBS+ Ventures, which released a "Marketing Intent Landscape," based on the LUMAscape charts. The idea is that intent doesn't exist solely in search, but in social, premium publishers, location-based marketing, ecommerce and video. "There has always been data in advertising and content. And the idea that intent-based marketing is new isn't true either. What is new and different is that we are entering an area where things are being much more easily shared by people, and we have the opportunity to communicate with them based on what they are sharing," KBS+ Director Taylor Davidson said. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0013hMI1i75d7Xp25HnObvZd2cJqi0_kx9-Y0YE2K2TCwDLvVl_aWZ4qbaucg__iF5g8B4Ac0eXspvK7xjzRe93hBa9r6ZxPkmUDxBLm5oRgPNQfFtuggVUArI9-cUTHHV-GpuUGIP450R5DhIyKu2mdk2Kx7KpGrOp13rc3DmQ5L0i6mm6ruXtC4uDvtXAjJjrEMJaHzTnq6VzjoCT_EY4kCKCHEWWXDX6UklCWoL62re5gD79OBIoH5q5df2_hL_b> .

 

Networked Native Ads

 

PandoDaily covers Nativo's announcement about new "premium" publishers using their native ads platform. James Freiman of new Nativo partner TheStreet says, "It's about both profitability and adding more quality content alongside our existing quality content. It doesn't work when the quality of an advertiser's editorial does it match up, but when you get the right content it can be highly lucrative. Nativo just makes it easier to do it at scale." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0013hMI1i75d7WbAj75eZMUGTQ4TP-D59GVn2vVlZt47MkZ0_6Bu9RgpQf64aqJ98fWQ9WSpW8lZHLEeatgQz1o8ymC_gsFuiYQaLUhIlM5lMCmJ7-InWis7FUbRvYVwYGb9M83QXMzv16rUfT-36-4PYwBmUl6030XJCBItmPgI1j_Fe902lfB8YeGPV4G_XACa1e0Z4O66tDDJ597LUHcLeIqe_b-nOna7oZrPrnmzLqdoyrdT62hJyC5G9WaFtqeaYsON5T_nuk=> .

 

Heart Of News

 

In his first lengthy interview on his acquisition of The Washington Post, Amazon CEO Jeff Bezos tells The Washington Post (what did you expect?) it will likely take years of experimentation to try and figure out WaPo's strategy going forward. He adds, "Whatever the mission, The Post will have readers at its centerpiece. I'm skeptical of any mission that has advertisers at its centerpiece. Whatever the mission is, it has news at its heart.'" Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0013hMI1i75d7WBs469YwLJO8FMHlPRfJ_Tf1DprnS0vfl1KVvKoYxMSLRAnWGkio9B1Q6-6Q8tVcOtW1Kkh6JxfYaboCmDg4ommQ7D-FdaFc5Rhd0GcpEoNNmG36gNGWEAelnNkqhCmKgZlqsfvcgjXGpgO5aWvq9iO7YlHIWxHbe-hcGyjjYbR_-L1rhqaE348HIDdAtKwKpHysWjuYHeZ_gYq6b91VSUl8lYzfgNzz9-sVUSmZRsW2_pPj6hx_oZ_41Uupwu4AkZsGsmj4cm23SjqMryhAN3uJzdiVONwCtsJ51DoqqogZ5GgUrgeM-Xurc8oH7I8ncyvW8xX1A8-T3eRFytM_MI> .

 

Cord Cutting, Day 4322

 

On Multichannel News, more data on cable subscribers potentially cutting the cord in favor of IP-based delivery. MN's Jeff Baumgartner covers SNL Kagan's research "that U.S. cable, satellite and telco TV providers lost a combined 366,000 video subscribers." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0013hMI1i75d7Vrjf4ffRA-g4i-2XDki-MrqMj-FM1lDyqoKjUhEeGgYQ9cwsnUA0B7EgZ3mGRNZdEpnaro5Mz1ckz2i2UbmcD_ZYnSWvBvjreeB7xjil4AYRs7rzofoXN2DZRv0Hw1C7Lui4qtCGPwEvnko6XACh0nJ7uFpzGCw8DGQsyaveYCFH56b3qwd0QuE6iqIX0p3okf560DT59Rm4kcW6QQKlOT> . The good news for cable jockeys is that year-over-year losses were better than in prior years.

The Technical CMO

 

Ivanka Trump poached Kate Spade's successful VP of ecommerce, Johanna Murphy, to transform her fashion line from wholesale to direct-to-consumer, Digiday reported. "When you look at traditional fashion brands that start in an offline way, their online presence, with the exception of a few, is weak; it still feels like an afterthought," Trump said in an interview. "It was really important that my CMO have digital experience, and she is the rare combination of being a true chief marketing officer, but not at the expense of not having a technical side." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0013hMI1i75d7VHB7iDGUw-q_nSWYDPzdEOqGSdSxjw5BIp2U5PbsnC4MqBu8nhiEHiXDHPTGiEv8z-GzDaqSPlhTmLOIOidNDJec9wpQqIVKOghKBaObcVm2zppxWAOAyarkDHOTxehcvuiDiFr5BtvIikQGErWGURnhwo0wlMVcssTny5sqS_5CFT8wd57IBXhl4RQKwemjDwGYR50ynh2w==> .

Video Ad Logistics

 

Facebook is pressing "auto-play" on its 15 second video ad strategy in users' newsfeeds in hopes of capturing TV and video ad budget. As the LA Times points out, however, the success of TV ads can largely be attributed to the fact that people are passively staring at a screen, not scrolling through a web page. "Video is the new black," said Tim Hanlon, founder and chief executive of the Vertere Group, an advertising consulting firm. "Everyone wants to do video, even if it doesn't seem to fit. And I think on its face video in social networks is a tough fit." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001l5sRI9Z1RTfeCasbmz7H6sRcAj3QEnYe6OhZShvDVn59qq87pXnMW2wnkCAN6D6_h6r0clTGK8A20M3bAhneRuI8RhKUVTH4GErlxRmBGHyaeIT4auH01FfcSxrkH87K4JpgbwxwSAYq25Okmiz5u3wBPXGorWXnS5h3DEsifxG2xHE9cHz5HMYOvlly-OBJIbGtstzz1a-3WBW3cVN9YQ==> . And then there's myth-debunking site Snopes.com which says <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001l5sRI9Z1RTd8v8Hoc81m7yV5Bqt-I29GqYJ0dX5FyJoJvlSFqKqVh5HGhD89MkmD3PW3y7y7J4ifTLjTe7Rnyg7wjkzqPQFN7d-w87gaSSeUwJnams_31WMNaCUlIfsmIu6f5gCZbik1dFZbkGcxyWyyGOPSMhPR>  FB video ads are still only "a claim."



Ecommerce Adding Media

 

Rakuten has plans that reach beyond traditional ecommerce as All Things D's Kara Swisher says that the company has acquired Viki, a video site she quotes as "Hulu for the rest of the world." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001l5sRI9Z1RTe9lKdVAj7IIyMAb4Gwc-Vty7Pn9U6cr7Nj01QvkY8oloe8zwzmBYuGIu4vbzVxYpiwOrhm6ZWzTnAsBB3_Q34oMxi9fAXxYPiAwcq1YsMi27J-cU8D09nT5n_aDOLBu3AW-R0ONEnyaIzvmdL7ut5xkV8Hm1SnmCOdMVJUpHQw82SggoAumEelnOFspSISKeFeyp3jL9LEdiu8XSF0Hwsf> . Rakuten CEO, Hiroshi Mikitani tells Swisher about the $200 million transaction: "Our foundation is not only limited to e-commerce, but an intention to strengthen our ecosystem in Japan and worldwide. We have been looking into finding a global solution for video." Is video ad tech next for Rakuten? It's affiliate marketing business - Rakuten Linkshare - bought retargeter Mediaforge in 2012 <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001l5sRI9Z1RTceW12zOPT5NoswdpG-edDFjWs2NMzTCkBcoCK2XRENPmwjRFtWXbzk1KOxR_eLNiA1kTo9S_SFqytsaU58Timwkxqi0qyEBP1kShWltdGe84OSZZ3gSV3ZS5b93659Zdq2GEXHitBJnpf4lOZf7mejwInsO-U3YVgfMl8Ut7MMBg==> .

 

Target Amps Up Mobile App

 

Target is the latest retail to begin tying its offline and online store through its mobile app, adding such features as in-store WiFi and localized shopping lists. Other enhancements, Mobile Commerce Daily is reporting, include a location-based weekly ad. All of these changes will help Target collect more data about consumers' shopping habits both online and in-store. It's still early days for this type of integration as a recent EKN Research study found only one in ten retailers have an in-store mode within an app. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001l5sRI9Z1RTdpsFKjZ-IYpA6vqBKN88MM_WBtl2YbH01IWm8EGroI5bFdp8DDb7qvdQ3Fie44P0CrlEJhJuw24zkDyTgZCk1WIv7ZGvSjuJhARjXxR3NckaXvqfgpimYfQY9oDuAIC-fSnUsK-GSVjEwoKcqQt2aaqfZwaAzhPH2M6BMiHVaylpsuhkGWtYobT5k7Vok3tbv8J_R-8aI2427Sxs8U-Viywr3SWyXk2nY=> .

 

Optimizing The Ad Network

 

TechCrunch's Anthony Ha gets a demo of a new mobile yield optimization product called Optimizer from MoPub. With the new product, he writes that the ad network "waterfall" is controlled by MoPub data rather than the data provided by ad networks, "Now, when publishers hit the Optimizer button, MoPub will automate that prioritization process based on its own data and the data it has acquired from various networks, so that it can predict the likely CPM, clickthrough rate, latency, and more on a given ad." Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001l5sRI9Z1RTd72mHtPNZGz2H1PI3ey7igC9o3LsxPD7FCwyEjAmmJF_xUQm5f_ZI46OCpWgzRZ5aiGLi-FHIGzsm3WwqXL-gfnt3-DMqc1v5MHWRpS7oW2bWUkll8Bc6_zKfrj3nngdzpEeWIGx2lxlDN7ojb2fWX> 

 

Completion Rates

 

Music streaming service Pandora has found success with video ads, according to ClickZ, despite the initial perception that it was just an audio platform. "We can say definitively that our auto-play video on Pandora is an effective driver throughout the entire consideration funnel from ad awareness through to brand consideration and purchase intent," claims Heidi Browning, SVP of strategic solutions at Pandora. "Our completion rates are very high and are well above the industry standard." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001l5sRI9Z1RTc0N7yBEvnNoBLljUgmLLQUanjulTH_4MMzujGzaJCLh8RsNHsnenmEx2mqBsCJnfY-d2xDED4yOSpY5A3nL2fWC9uzlmwe4kMe-zvoneuskkHfyw6wykzgOWcF9i6w903T60jJdmBxOfKTWOM-68jvWvf0-SfaOIOA3ANv2mT7sbjOVAdaKrqtkzbfrYU7Q8Hw4v5m1KloIg==> .

Pinterest Data

 

After Pinterest opened up its network to be more business friendly, companies have been flexing their viral marketing muscles on the social platform. Examples include exclusive giveaways and product launches. ReadWrite's Lauren Orsini examined the way hotel chain Four Seasons is using the site to act as a concierge service through its Pin.Pack.Go promotion. All it requires is a basic understanding of Pinterest and everything else is handled by the hotel. Read more about it here <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001l5sRI9Z1RTd6RI6Asv2ajngUwlW2uzB6fSq6EbQESWxAxQDHtT-xgomAx3b1yXcwOd-GHga8t1AFP_QZ91pgUpNyk1Cq9ueQtU6t5qchTy7CyXFAiXkzyl9SQa8lyyMdKcEmVk4dkVT2nAKb8CPNmJ8a1DiLoNdjcaQFLoaNr42VSEAcTbCXAPJbFhTJJwj0KC0NSiGxB_T1tXQXsxixfVZS-ldcvfKJu8v_TIKcZ6s=> . Pinterest data is waiting to be unlocked.. it's only a matter of time.



The New Media Model



Joe Marchese, CEO of SocialVibe, takes to Ad Age and explains in the wake of the Publicis Omnicom Merger why the combined entity's buying clout won't result in lower rates for publishers and the like. He points to digital where premium publishers are putting up paywalls, streaming services like Pandora and Netflix are offering paid subscriptions without ads and DVR technology is allowing consumers to skip right over ads. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001l5sRI9Z1RTcTXUOR30Y3ASjgXFlcOyruXt2aT57ZouzsUKpUxIOkbqYglgS58X09webt282Fs7Pme1K_nDEMCXTYC-b7RBmDmQdZEk8880myRsUwmyp_A0-f0Z5WM0Drkd3qoVoiJSV1uebHhnY88HosrC1o38WmUh0vgaWRkhkKgBtErfvzIsDlkDx1UiWarvw4zNYty7k=> .

 

Shoveling Display

 

The Wall Street Journal covers this success of what may be one of the few newspapers not in decline - the Amish newspapers Budget and Die Botschaft. No need for brand safety filters here! At Die Botschaft "photos of people aren't allowed in ads. Shovel photos are permitted. The ad for Smuckers Horse Dentistry shows a drawing of two horses. The more lenient Budget, meanwhile, ran an ad with a photo of an 87-year-old grandmother providing a testimonial for a pill that helped stop her itching within three days..." Read it (subscription). <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001l5sRI9Z1RTf8n35s7hs2XV7jJSfjPYZSUeCyBKQEiBIu0Nt3i5w8aRK7gAMeR0atAIryDR_2OW-XZ730sHHOg5Fkk2nHUvsDzgYeUA7YeDvvL-MBtkghFKNipcFcLjFvKGfx6XJxw3dyJgwhRBlinKfazoizzHHjL-7l64kWcGAT6ykOKhy5g0O8MAMdReF9>
